<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Recognition">Recognition</span></h2>
<ul><li>In 1987, Gates was listed as a billionaire in <i><a href="/wiki/Forbes" title="Forbes">Forbes</a></i> magazine's 400 Richest People in America issue. He was worth $1.25&#160;billion and was the world's youngest self-made billionaire.<sup id="cite_ref-FORBES_The_Next_Bill_Gates_15-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FORBES_The_Next_Bill_Gates-15">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> Since 1987, Gates has been included in the <i>Forbes</i> <a href="/wiki/The_World%27s_Billionaires" title="The World&#39;s Billionaires">The World's Billionaires</a> list and was the wealthiest from 1995 to 1996,<sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137">&#91;135&#93;</a></sup> 1998 to 2007, 2009, and held the spot until 2018 before being overtaken by <a href="/wiki/Jeff_Bezos" title="Jeff Bezos">Jeff Bezos</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Forbes_profile_16-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Forbes_profile-16">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> Gates was number one on the <a href="/wiki/Forbes_400" title="Forbes 400">Forbes 400</a> list from 1993 through to 2007, 2009, and 2014 through 2017.<sup id="cite_ref-Wahba_138-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Wahba-138">&#91;136&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-139" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-139">&#91;137&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i>Time</i> magazine named Gates <a href="/wiki/Time_100:_The_Most_Important_People_of_the_Century#The_only_people_to_shape_both_the_20th_century_and_the_early_21st" title="Time 100: The Most Important People of the Century">one of the 100 people who most influenced the 20th century</a>, as well as <a href="/wiki/Time_100" title="Time 100">one of the 100 most influential people</a> of 2004, 2005, and 2006.</li>
<li><i>Time</i> also collectively named Gates, his wife Melinda and U2's lead singer <a href="/wiki/Bono" title="Bono">Bono</a> as the 2005 <a href="/wiki/Time_Magazine_Person_of_the_Year" class="mw-redirect" title="Time Magazine Person of the Year">Persons of the Year</a> for their humanitarian efforts.<sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140">&#91;138&#93;</a></sup> In 2006, he was voted eighth in the list of "Heroes of our time".<sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141">&#91;139&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Gates was listed in the London <i><a href="/wiki/Sunday_Times" class="mw-redirect" title="Sunday Times">Sunday Times</a></i> power list in 1999, named CEO of the year by <i>Chief Executive Officers magazine</i> in 1994, ranked number one in the "Top 50 Cyber Elite" by <i>Time</i> in 1998, ranked number two in the <i><a href="/wiki/Upside_(magazine)" title="Upside (magazine)">Upside</a></i> Elite 100 in 1999, and was included in <i><a href="/wiki/The_Guardian" title="The Guardian">The Guardian</a></i> as one of the "Top 100 influential people in media" in 2001.<sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142">&#91;140&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Gates was elected Member of the US <a href="/wiki/National_Academy_of_Engineering" title="National Academy of Engineering">National Academy of Engineering</a> in 1996 "for contributions to the founding and development of personal computing".<sup id="cite_ref-143" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-143">&#91;141&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>He was named Honorary Member of the <a href="/wiki/American_Library_Association" title="American Library Association">American Library Association</a> in 1998.<sup id="cite_ref-144" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-144">&#91;142&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>He was elected a foreign member of the <a href="/wiki/Chinese_Academy_of_Engineering" title="Chinese Academy of Engineering">Chinese Academy of Engineering</a> in 2017.<sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145">&#91;143&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>According to <i>Forbes</i>, Gates was ranked as the fourth most powerful person in the world in 2012,<sup id="cite_ref-146" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-146">&#91;144&#93;</a></sup> up from fifth in 2011.<sup id="cite_ref-147" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-147">&#91;145&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>In 1994, he was honored as the 20th <a href="/wiki/Distinguished_Fellow_of_the_British_Computer_Society" title="Distinguished Fellow of the British Computer Society">Distinguished Fellow of the British Computer Society</a> (DFBCS). In 1999, Gates received <a href="/wiki/New_York_Institute_of_Technology" title="New York Institute of Technology">New York Institute of Technology</a>'s President's Medal.<sup id="cite_ref-148" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-148">&#91;146&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Gates has received honorary doctorates from <a href="/wiki/Nyenrode_Business_Universiteit" class="mw-redirect" title="Nyenrode Business Universiteit">Nyenrode Business Universiteit</a> (2003),<sup id="cite_ref-149" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-149">&#91;147&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/KTH_Royal_Institute_of_Technology" title="KTH Royal Institute of Technology">KTH Royal Institute of Technology</a> (2002),<sup id="cite_ref-150" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-150">&#91;148&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Waseda_University" title="Waseda University">Waseda University</a> (2005),<sup id="cite_ref-151" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-151">&#91;149&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Tsinghua_University" title="Tsinghua University">Tsinghua University</a> (2007),<sup id="cite_ref-152" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-152">&#91;150&#93;</a></sup> Harvard University (2007),<sup id="cite_ref-153" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-153">&#91;151&#93;</a></sup> the <a href="/wiki/Karolinska_Institute" title="Karolinska Institute">Karolinska Institute</a> (2007),<sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154">&#91;152&#93;</a></sup> and Cambridge University (2009).<sup id="cite_ref-155" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-155">&#91;153&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>He was also made an honorary trustee of <a href="/wiki/Peking_University" title="Peking University">Peking University</a> in 2007.<sup id="cite_ref-156" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-156">&#91;154&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Gates was made an Honorary <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_British_Empire" title="Order of the British Empire">Knight Commander of the Order of the British Empire</a> (KBE) by Queen <a href="/wiki/Elizabeth_II" title="Elizabeth II">Elizabeth II</a> in 2005.<sup id="cite_ref-157" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-157">&#91;155&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>In January 2006, he was awarded the Grand Cross of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_Prince_Henry" title="Order of Prince Henry">Order of Prince Henry</a> by the President of Portugal <a href="/wiki/Jorge_Sampaio" title="Jorge Sampaio">Jorge Sampaio</a></li>
<li>In November 2006, he was awarded the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Aztec_Eagle" title="Order of the Aztec Eagle">Placard of the Order of the Aztec Eagle</a>, together with his wife Melinda who was awarded the Insignia of the same order, both for their philanthropic work around the world in the areas of health and education, particularly in Mexico, and specifically in the program "<i><i lang="es" title="Spanish-language text">Un país de lectores</i></i>".<sup id="cite_ref-158" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-158">&#91;156&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Gates received the 2010 <a href="/wiki/Bower_Award_for_Business_Leadership" class="mw-redirect" title="Bower Award for Business Leadership">Bower Award for Business Leadership</a> from <a href="/wiki/The_Franklin_Institute" class="mw-redirect" title="The Franklin Institute">The Franklin Institute</a> for his achievements at Microsoft and his philanthropic work.<sup id="cite_ref-159" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-159">&#91;157&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Also in 2010, he was honored with the <a href="/wiki/Silver_Buffalo_Award" title="Silver Buffalo Award">Silver Buffalo Award</a> by the <a href="/wiki/Boy_Scouts_of_America" title="Boy Scouts of America">Boy Scouts of America</a>, its highest award for adults, for his service to youth.<sup id="cite_ref-SB2010_160-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SB2010-160">&#91;158&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>In 2002, Bill and Melinda Gates received the <a href="/wiki/Jefferson_Awards_for_Public_Service" title="Jefferson Awards for Public Service">Jefferson Award</a> for Greatest Public Service Benefiting the Disadvantaged.<sup id="cite_ref-161" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-161">&#91;159&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>He was given the 2006 James C. Morgan Global Humanitarian Award from <a href="/wiki/The_Tech_Awards" title="The Tech Awards">the Tech Awards</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-162" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-162">&#91;160&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>In 2015, Gates and his wife Melinda received the <a href="/wiki/Padma_Bhushan" title="Padma Bhushan">Padma Bhushan</a>, India's third-highest civilian award for their social work in the country.<sup id="cite_ref-163" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-163">&#91;161&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-164" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-164">&#91;162&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> honored Bill and Melinda Gates with the <a href="/wiki/Presidential_Medal_of_Freedom" title="Presidential Medal of Freedom">Presidential Medal of Freedom</a> for their philanthropic efforts in 2016,<sup id="cite_ref-165" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-165">&#91;163&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Fran%C3%A7ois_Hollande" title="François Hollande">François Hollande</a> awarded Bill and Melinda in the following year with France's highest national order – as Commander of the <a href="/wiki/Legion_of_Honour" title="Legion of Honour">Legion of Honour</a> for their charity efforts.<sup id="cite_ref-166" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-166">&#91;164&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Entomology" title="Entomology">Entomologists</a> named <a href="/wiki/Bill_Gates%27_flower_fly" title="Bill Gates&#39; flower fly">Bill Gates' flower fly</a>, <i><i lang="la" title="Latin-language text">Eristalis gatesi</i></i>, in his honor in 1997.<sup id="cite_ref-167" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-167">&#91;165&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Bill_og_Melinda_Gates_2009-06-03_(bilde_01).JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/28/Bill_og_Melinda_Gates_2009-06-03_%28bilde_01%29.JPG/220px-Bill_og_Melinda_Gates_2009-06-03_%28bilde_01%29.JPG" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/28/Bill_og_Melinda_Gates_2009-06-03_%28bilde_01%29.JPG/330px-Bill_og_Melinda_Gates_2009-06-03_%28bilde_01%29.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/28/Bill_og_Melinda_Gates_2009-06-03_%28bilde_01%29.JPG/440px-Bill_og_Melinda_Gates_2009-06-03_%28bilde_01%29.JPG 2x" data-file-width="2808" data-file-height="1872" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Bill_og_Melinda_Gates_2009-06-03_(bilde_01).JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Gates and his wife, <a href="/wiki/Melinda_Gates" title="Melinda Gates">Melinda</a>, 2009</div></div></div>
<p>Gates married <a href="/wiki/Melinda_Gates" title="Melinda Gates">Melinda French</a> on a golf course on the Hawaiian island of <a href="/wiki/Lanai" title="Lanai">Lanai</a> on January 1, 1994. They have three children. The family's <a href="/wiki/Bill_Gates%27s_house" title="Bill Gates&#39;s house">residence</a> is an <a href="/wiki/Earth_sheltering" class="mw-redirect" title="Earth sheltering">earth-sheltered mansion</a> in the side of a hill overlooking <a href="/wiki/Lake_Washington" title="Lake Washington">Lake Washington</a> in <a href="/wiki/Medina,_Washington" title="Medina, Washington">Medina, Washington</a>. In 2009, <a href="/wiki/Property_tax" title="Property tax">property taxes</a> on the mansion were reported to be US$1.063&#160;million, on a total assessed value of US$147.5&#160;million.<sup id="cite_ref-168" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-168">&#91;166&#93;</a></sup> The 66,000-square-foot (6,100&#160;m<sup>2</sup>) estate has a 60-foot (18&#160;m) swimming pool with an underwater music system, as well as a 2,500-square-foot (230&#160;m<sup>2</sup>) gym and a 1,000-square-foot (93&#160;m<sup>2</sup>) dining room.<sup id="cite_ref-169" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-169">&#91;167&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In an interview with <i><a href="/wiki/Rolling_Stone" title="Rolling Stone">Rolling Stone</a></i>, Gates stated in regard to his faith: "The moral systems of religion, I think, are super important. We've raised our kids in a religious way; they've gone to the Catholic church that Melinda goes to and I participate in. I've been very lucky, and therefore I owe it to try and reduce the inequity in the world. And that's kind of a religious belief. I mean, it's at least a moral belief."<sup id="cite_ref-God_170-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-God-170">&#91;168&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Gates also said: "I agree with people like <a href="/wiki/Richard_Dawkins" title="Richard Dawkins">Richard Dawkins</a> that mankind felt the need for creation myths. Before we really began to understand disease and the weather and things like that, we sought false explanations for them. Now science has filled in some of the realm&#160;– not all&#160;– that religion used to fill. But the mystery and the beauty of the world is overwhelmingly amazing, and there's no scientific explanation of how it came about. To say that it was generated by random numbers, that does seem, you know, sort of an uncharitable view [laughs]. I think it makes sense to believe in God, but exactly what decision in your life you make differently because of it, I don't know."<sup id="cite_ref-God_170-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-God-170">&#91;168&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Gates purchased the <a href="/wiki/Codex_Leicester" title="Codex Leicester">Codex Leicester</a>, a collection of scientific writings by <a href="/wiki/Leonardo_da_Vinci" title="Leonardo da Vinci">Leonardo da Vinci</a>, for US$30.8&#160;million at an auction in 1994.<sup id="cite_ref-171" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-171">&#91;169&#93;</a></sup> Gates is an avid reader, and the ceiling of his large home library is engraved with a quotation from <i><a href="/wiki/The_Great_Gatsby" title="The Great Gatsby">The Great Gatsby</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-172" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-172">&#91;170&#93;</a></sup> He also enjoys playing bridge, tennis, and golf.<sup id="cite_ref-173" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-173">&#91;171&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-174" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-174">&#91;172&#93;</a></sup> Gates's days are planned for him on a minute-by-minute basis, similar to the <a href="/wiki/U.S._President" class="mw-redirect" title="U.S. President">U.S. President</a>'s schedule.<sup id="cite_ref-175" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-175">&#91;173&#93;</a></sup> Despite his wealth and extensive business travel, Gates flew <a href="/wiki/Coach_class" class="mw-redirect" title="Coach class">coach</a> in <a href="/wiki/Commercial_aircraft" class="mw-redirect" title="Commercial aircraft">commercial aircraft</a> until 1997, when he bought a private jet.
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:170217-D-GO396-0147_(32577063650).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1e/170217-D-GO396-0147_%2832577063650%29.jpg/220px-170217-D-GO396-0147_%2832577063650%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1e/170217-D-GO396-0147_%2832577063650%29.jpg/330px-170217-D-GO396-0147_%2832577063650%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1e/170217-D-GO396-0147_%2832577063650%29.jpg/440px-170217-D-GO396-0147_%2832577063650%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3982" data-file-height="2655" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:170217-D-GO396-0147_(32577063650).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Gates meets with U.S. Secretary of Defense <a href="/wiki/James_Mattis" class="mw-redirect" title="James Mattis">James Mattis</a>, February 2017</div></div></div>
<p>In 1999, his wealth briefly surpassed US$101&#160;billion.<sup id="cite_ref-176" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-176">&#91;174&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-zuckerman19971027_177-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-zuckerman19971027-177">&#91;175&#93;</a></sup> Since 2000, the nominal value of his Microsoft holdings has declined due to a fall in Microsoft's stock price after the <a href="/wiki/Dot-com_bubble" title="Dot-com bubble">dot-com bubble</a> burst and the multi-billion dollar donations he has made to his charitable foundations. In May 2006, Gates remarked that he wished that he were not the richest man in the world because he disliked the attention it brought.<sup id="cite_ref-178" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-178">&#91;176&#93;</a></sup> In March 2010, Gates was the second wealthiest person behind <a href="/wiki/Carlos_Slim" title="Carlos Slim">Carlos Slim</a>, but regained the top position in 2013, according to the Bloomberg Billionaires List.<sup id="cite_ref-Bloom_179-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Bloom-179">&#91;177&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-180" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-180">&#91;178&#93;</a></sup> Slim retook the position again in June 2014<sup id="cite_ref-wealthy_list_181-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-wealthy_list-181">&#91;179&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-New_wealthiest_man_182-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-New_wealthiest_man-182">&#91;180&#93;</a></sup> (but then lost the top position back to Gates). Between 2009 and 2014, his wealth doubled from US$40&#160;billion to more than US$82&#160;billion.<sup id="cite_ref-183" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-183">&#91;181&#93;</a></sup> In October 2017, Gates was surpassed by <a href="/wiki/Amazon_(company)" title="Amazon (company)">Amazon</a> founder <a href="/wiki/Jeff_Bezos" title="Jeff Bezos">Jeff Bezos</a> as the richest person in the world.<sup id="cite_ref-Forbes_17-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Forbes-17">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> On November 15, 2019, he once again became the richest person in the world after a 48% increase in Microsoft shares, surpassing Bezos.<sup id="cite_ref-:3_184-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:3-184">&#91;182&#93;</a></sup> Gates told the <a href="/wiki/BBC" title="BBC">BBC</a>, "I've paid more tax than any individual ever, and gladly so&#160;... I've paid over $6 billion in taxes."<sup id="cite_ref-185" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-185">&#91;183&#93;</a></sup> He is a proponent of higher taxes, particularly for the rich.<sup id="cite_ref-186" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-186">&#91;184&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Gates has held the top spot on the list of <i><a href="/wiki/The_World%27s_Billionaires" title="The World&#39;s Billionaires">The World's Billionaires</a></i> for 18 out of the past 23 years.<sup id="cite_ref-187" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-187">&#91;185&#93;</a></sup> Gates has several investments outside Microsoft, which in 2006 paid him a salary of US$616,667 and US$350,000 bonus totalling US$966,667.<sup id="cite_ref-188" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-188">&#91;186&#93;</a></sup> In 1989, he founded <a href="/wiki/Branded_Entertainment_Network" title="Branded Entertainment Network">Corbis</a>, a digital imaging company. In 2004, he became a director of <a href="/wiki/Berkshire_Hathaway" title="Berkshire Hathaway">Berkshire Hathaway</a>, the investment company headed by long-time friend <a href="/wiki/Warren_Buffett" title="Warren Buffett">Warren Buffett</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-189" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-189">&#91;187&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In 2016, he revealed that he is <a href="/wiki/Color_blindness" title="Color blindness">color-blind</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-190" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-190">&#91;188&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="External_business_ventures_and_investments_.28partial_list.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="External_business_ventures_and_investments_(partial_list)">External business ventures and investments (partial list)</span></h3>
<p>Gates has a multi-billion dollar investment portfolio with stake in various sectors<sup id="cite_ref-191" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-191">&#91;189&#93;</a></sup> and has participated in several entrepreneurial ventures beyond Microsoft, including:
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/AutoNation" title="AutoNation">AutoNation</a>, automotive retailer that Gates has a 16% stake in trading on the <a href="/wiki/NYSE" class="mw-redirect" title="NYSE">NYSE</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/BgC3" title="BgC3">bgC3</a>, a new think-tank company founded by Gates.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Canadian_National_Railway" title="Canadian National Railway">Canadian National Railway (CN)</a>, a Canadian <a href="/wiki/Class_I_railroad" class="mw-redirect" title="Class I railroad">Class I freight railway</a>. As of 2019, Bill Gates is the largest single shareholder of CN stock.<sup id="cite_ref-CBC_192-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CBC-192">&#91;190&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Cascade_Investment" title="Cascade Investment">Cascade Investment</a> LLC, a private investment and holding company incorporated in the United States, founded and controlled by Bill Gates and headquartered in <a href="/wiki/Kirkland,_Washington" title="Kirkland, Washington">Kirkland, Washington</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Branded_Entertainment_Network" title="Branded Entertainment Network">Corbis</a> (originally named Interactive Home Systems and now known as Branded Entertainment Network), a digital image licensing and rights services company founded by Gates.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/EarthNow" title="EarthNow">EarthNow</a>, Seattle-based startup company aiming to blanket the Earth with live satellite video coverage. Gates is a large financial backer.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Eclipse_Aviation" title="Eclipse Aviation">Eclipse Aviation</a>, a defunct manufacturer of <a href="/wiki/Very_light_jets" class="mw-redirect" title="Very light jets">very light jets</a>. Gates was a major stake-holder early on in the project.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ecolab" title="Ecolab">Ecolab</a>, global provider of water, hygiene and energy technologies and services to the food, energy, healthcare, industrial and hospitality markets. Gates increased his stake of 10.8% in Ecolab to 25% in 2012.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/ResearchGate" title="ResearchGate">ResearchGate</a>, a social networking site for scientists. Gates participated in a $35&#160;million round of financing along with other investors.<sup id="cite_ref-193" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-193">&#91;191&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/TerraPower" title="TerraPower">TerraPower</a>, a nuclear reactor design company founded by Gates.</li></ul>
<p>Gates is the top private owner of farmland in the United States with landholdings totaling 242,000 acres across 19 states, and the 49th largest private owner of land.<sup id="cite_ref-194" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-194">&#91;192&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-195" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-195">&#91;193&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="In_media">In media</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Books">Books</span></h3>
<p>Gates has written three books:
</p>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Road_Ahead_(Bill_Gates_book)" class="mw-redirect" title="The Road Ahead (Bill Gates book)">The Road Ahead</a></i>, written with Microsoft executive <a href="/wiki/Nathan_Myhrvold" title="Nathan Myhrvold">Nathan Myhrvold</a> and journalist <a href="/wiki/Peter_Rinearson" title="Peter Rinearson">Peter Rinearson</a>, was published in November 1995. It summarized the implications of the personal computing revolution and described a future profoundly changed by the arrival of a global <a href="/wiki/Information_superhighway" title="Information superhighway">information superhighway</a>.</li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Business_@_the_Speed_of_Thought" title="Business @ the Speed of Thought">Business @ the Speed of Thought</a></i> was published in 1999, and discusses how business and technology are integrated, and shows how digital infrastructures and information networks can help to get an edge on the competition.</li>
<li><i>How to Avoid a Climate Disaster</i> (February 2021) presents what Gates learned in over a decade of studying climate change and investing in innovations to address climate problems.</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Video_game">Video game</span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/DONKEY.BAS" title="DONKEY.BAS">DONKEY.BAS</a>, is a <a href="/wiki/Computer_game" class="mw-redirect" title="Computer game">computer game</a> written in 1981 and included with early versions of the PC DOS operating system distributed with the original IBM PC. It is a <a href="/wiki/Driving_game" class="mw-redirect" title="Driving game">driving game</a> in which the <a href="/wiki/Player_character" title="Player character">player</a> must avoid hitting <a href="/wiki/Donkey" title="Donkey">donkeys</a>. The game was written by Bill Gates and <a href="/wiki/Neil_Konzen" title="Neil Konzen">Neil Konzen</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-196" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-196">&#91;194&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-197" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-197">&#91;195&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Documentary_films_about_Gates">Documentary films about Gates</span></h3>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 210px; float: right; clear: right; margin:0 0 1.5em 1.5em"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold;font-size:115%">External video</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;text-align: left"><img alt="video icon" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Nuvola_apps_kaboodle.svg/16px-Nuvola_apps_kaboodle.svg.png" decoding="async" width="16" height="16" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Nuvola_apps_kaboodle.svg/24px-Nuvola_apps_kaboodle.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Nuvola_apps_kaboodle.svg/32px-Nuvola_apps_kaboodle.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://openvault.wgbh.org/catalog/V_7C97C4381B7849D791CD357588C2FE89">The Machine That Changed The World; Interview with Bill Gates, 1990</a> (raw video), 44:03, <a href="/wiki/WGBH_Educational_Foundation" title="WGBH Educational Foundation">Open Vault WGBH</a><sup id="cite_ref-wgbhov_198-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-wgbhov-198">&#91;196&#93;</a></sup></td></tr></tbody></table>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/The_Machine_That_Changed_the_World_(miniseries)" title="The Machine That Changed the World (miniseries)"><i>The Machine That Changed the World</i></a> (1990)</li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Triumph_of_the_Nerds" title="Triumph of the Nerds">Triumph of the Nerds</a></i> (1996)</li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Nerds_2.0.1" title="Nerds 2.0.1">Nerds 2.0.1</a></i> (1998)</li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Waiting_for_%22Superman%22" title="Waiting for &quot;Superman&quot;">Waiting for "Superman"</a></i> (2010)<sup id="cite_ref-199" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-199">&#91;197&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Virtual_Revolution" title="The Virtual Revolution">The Virtual Revolution</a></i> (2010)</li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Inside_Bill%27s_Brain:_Decoding_Bill_Gates" title="Inside Bill&#39;s Brain: Decoding Bill Gates">Inside Bill's Brain: Decoding Bill Gates</a></i> (2019)</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Feature_films">Feature films</span></h3>
<ul><li>1999: <i><a href="/wiki/Pirates_of_Silicon_Valley" title="Pirates of Silicon Valley">Pirates of Silicon Valley</a></i>, a film that chronicles the rise of <a href="/wiki/Apple_Inc." title="Apple Inc.">Apple</a> and <a href="/wiki/Microsoft" title="Microsoft">Microsoft</a> from the early 1970s to 1997. Gates is portrayed by <a href="/wiki/Anthony_Michael_Hall" title="Anthony Michael Hall">Anthony Michael Hall</a>.</li>
<li>2002: <i><a href="/wiki/Nothing_So_Strange" title="Nothing So Strange">Nothing So Strange</a></i>, a mockumentary featuring Gates as the subject of a modern assassination. Gates briefly appears at the start, played by Steve Sires.</li>
<li>2010: <i><a href="/wiki/The_Social_Network" title="The Social Network">The Social Network</a>,</i> a film that chronicles the development of <a href="/wiki/Facebook" title="Facebook">Facebook</a>. Gates is portrayed by Steve Sires.<sup id="cite_ref-200" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-200">&#91;198&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>2015: <i><a href="/wiki/Steve_Jobs" title="Steve Jobs">Steve Jobs</a> vs. Bill Gates: The Competition to Control the Personal Computer, 1974–1999</i>: Original film from the <a href="/wiki/National_Geographic_Channel" class="mw-redirect" title="National Geographic Channel">National Geographic Channel</a> for the <i><a href="/wiki/American_Genius" title="American Genius">American Genius</a></i> series.<sup id="cite_ref-201" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-201">&#91;199&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Video_and_film_clips">Video and film clips</span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Steve_Jobs_and_Bill_Gates_(522695099).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/Steve_Jobs_and_Bill_Gates_%28522695099%29.jpg/220px-Steve_Jobs_and_Bill_Gates_%28522695099%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="157" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/Steve_Jobs_and_Bill_Gates_%28522695099%29.jpg/330px-Steve_Jobs_and_Bill_Gates_%28522695099%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/Steve_Jobs_and_Bill_Gates_%28522695099%29.jpg/440px-Steve_Jobs_and_Bill_Gates_%28522695099%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3076" data-file-height="2194" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Steve_Jobs_and_Bill_Gates_(522695099).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Steve_Jobs" title="Steve Jobs">Steve Jobs</a> and Gates at <a href="/wiki/All_Things_Digital" title="All Things Digital"><i>D: All Things Digital</i></a> in 2007</div></div></div>
<ul><li>1983: Steve Jobs hosts Bill Gates in the Macintosh dating game at the Macintosh pre-launch event (with <a href="/wiki/Steve_Jobs" title="Steve Jobs">Steve Jobs</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mitch_Kapor" title="Mitch Kapor">Mitch Kapor</a>, references the television show, <i><a href="/wiki/The_Dating_Game" title="The Dating Game">The Dating Game</a></i>)</li>
<li>2007: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=wvhW8cp15tk">Steve Jobs and Bill Gates Together at the D5 Conference</a>, <i><a href="/wiki/All_Things_Digital" title="All Things Digital">All Things Digital</a></i></li>
<li>2009−&#160;: Bill Gates has given numerous <a href="/wiki/TED_(Conference)" class="mw-redirect" title="TED (Conference)">TED talks</a> on current concerns such as innovation, education and fighting global diseases<sup id="cite_ref-202" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-202">&#91;200&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Radio">Radio</span></h3>
<p>Gates was the guest on <a href="/wiki/BBC_Radio_4" title="BBC Radio 4">BBC Radio 4</a>'s <i><a href="/wiki/Desert_Island_Discs" title="Desert Island Discs">Desert Island Discs</a></i> on January 31, 2016, in which he talked about his relationships with his <a href="/wiki/William_H._Gates_Sr." class="mw-redirect" title="William H. Gates Sr.">father</a> and <a href="/wiki/Steve_Jobs" title="Steve Jobs">Steve Jobs</a>, meeting <a href="/wiki/Melinda_Gates" title="Melinda Gates">Melinda Ann French</a>, the start of <a href="/wiki/Microsoft" title="Microsoft">Microsoft</a> and some of his habits (for example reading <i><a href="/wiki/The_Economist" title="The Economist">The Economist</a></i> "from cover to cover every week"). His choice of things to take on a desert island were, for music: "<a href="/wiki/Blue_Skies_(Irving_Berlin_song)" title="Blue Skies (Irving Berlin song)">Blue Skies</a>" by <a href="/wiki/Willie_Nelson" title="Willie Nelson">Willie Nelson</a>; a book: <i><a href="/wiki/The_Better_Angels_of_Our_Nature" title="The Better Angels of Our Nature">The Better Angels of Our Nature</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Steven_Pinker" title="Steven Pinker">Steven Pinker</a>; and luxury item: a DVD Collection of Lectures from <a href="/wiki/The_Teaching_Company" class="mw-redirect" title="The Teaching Company">The Teaching Company</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-203" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-203">&#91;201&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Television">Television</span></h3>
<p>Gates made a guest appearance as himself on the <a href="/wiki/Emmy_Award" title="Emmy Award">Emmy Award</a> winning TV show <i><a href="/wiki/The_Big_Bang_Theory" title="The Big Bang Theory">The Big Bang Theory</a></i>. The episode on which he appeared was appropriately entitled "<a href="/wiki/The_Big_Bang_Theory_(season_11)" title="The Big Bang Theory (season 11)">The Gates Excitation</a>."<sup id="cite_ref-204" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-204">&#91;202&#93;</a></sup> He also appeared in a cameo role in 2019 on the series finale of <i><a href="/wiki/Silicon_Valley_(TV_series)" title="Silicon Valley (TV series)">Silicon Valley</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-205" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-205">&#91;203&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<li id="cite_note-7"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-7">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Gates regularly documents his share ownership through public U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission <a href="/wiki/Form_4" title="Form 4">form 4</a> filings.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-21"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-21">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">His father was named William H. Gates II, but he is now generally known as William H. Gates, Senior to avoid confusion with his son.</span>
</li>
</ol></div></div>
